CREATE TABLE Scoreboard ( game_id INT, player_id INT, score INT, level INT, PRIMARY KEY (game_id, player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );

CREATE TABLE Player ( player_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_name VARCHAR(255), email VARCHAR(255), date_of_birth DATE, country VARCHAR(50) );

CREATE TABLE GameReview ( review_id INT PRIMARY KEY, game_id INT, player_id INT, rating FLOAT, review_text TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );</t><s>alter table game add column publisher varchar(255);</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE Game ( game_id INT PRIMARY KEY, title VARCHAR(255), genre VARCHAR(50), release_date DATE, platform VARCHAR(50) );

CREATE TABLE Scoreboard ( game_id INT, player_id INT, score INT, level INT, PRIMARY KEY (game_id, player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );

CREATE TABLE GameReview ( review_id INT PRIMARY KEY, game_id INT, player_id INT, rating FLOAT, review_text TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );</t><s>ALTER TABLE Player ADD COLUMN age INT;</s>

CREATE TABLE PlayerGameHistory (PlayerID INT, GameID INT, PlayTimeInHours INT, Score INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID), FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID));

CREATE TABLE GameReview (ReviewID INT PRIMARY KEY, GameID INT, PlayerID INT, Rating INT, ReviewText TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID), FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));</t><s>alter table game add column publisher varchar(50);</s>

CREATE TABLE PlayerInventory (InventoryID INT PRIMARY KEY, PlayerID INT, ItemName VARCHAR(50), Quantity INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));</t><s>ALTER TABLE Game ADD COLUMN Publisher VARCHAR(50);</s>

CREATE TABLE Player (PlayerID INT PRIMARY KEY, PlayerName VARCHAR(50), Age INT, Email VARCHAR(50), HighScore INT);
